<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́ть</a> (4079)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:играть.html>игра́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">igrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проиграть.html>проигра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proigrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрывать.html>прои́грывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lose</li>
<li>to play, to play through, to play over</li></ol>

***проигрыватель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыватель.html>прои́грыватель</a> (22349)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрывать.html>прои́грывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proígryvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыватель.html>прои́грыватель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proígryvatelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыватель.html>прои́грывателя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыватель.html>прои́грыватели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыватель.html>прои́грывателей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>gramophone, record player</li>
<li>(media) player (e.g. CD, DVD, mp3)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:граммофон.html>граммофо́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">grammofón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">электрофо́н</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">elektrofón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***проигрыш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыш.html>про́игрыш</a> (15495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыш.html>про́игрыш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próigryš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыш.html>про́игрыша</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыш.html>про́игрыши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проигрыш.html>про́игрышей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loss, losing <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a game or war</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>loss, what is lost, the lost sum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> musical part of a song without singing</li></ol>

***произвести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a> (1918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proizvestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make, to carry out, to execute, to effect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proizvestí</b> remónt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to repair, to carry out repairs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give birth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proizvestí</b> na svet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring into the world; to give birth (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to produce</li>
<li>to promote</li>
<li>to cause, to produce, to create</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a> (2279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proizvodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвести.html>произвести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make, to carry out, to execute, to effect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proizvodítʹ</b> remónt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to repair, to carry out repairs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give birth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:производить.html>производи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proizvodítʹ</b> na svet</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring into the world; to give birth (to)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to promote</li>
<li>to cause, to produce, to create</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произвол.html>произво́л</a> (8806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвол.html>произво́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proizvól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвол.html>произво́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвол.html>произво́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвол.html>произво́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>free will</li>
<li>power abuse; arbitrary will, behaviour or rule</li>
<li>lawlessness</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвольный.html>произво́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proizvólʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произвольный.html>произво́льно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proizvólʹno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>arbitrarily, randomly</li>
<li>ad hoc <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">on the spur of the moment</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***произнёсший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произнести.html>произнёсший</a> (565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***произнести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произнести.html>произнести́</a> (565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">изнести́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произнести.html>произнести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proiznestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произносить.html>произноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pronounce, to articulate</li>
<li>to deliver, to utter</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произносить.html>произноси́ть</a> (2314)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:износить.html>износи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">частичн.</span>: произнесение</li>

***произойти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произойти́</a> (474)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изойти.html>изойти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izojtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произойти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proizojtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происходить.html>происходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take place, to happen, to occur</li>
<li>to derive, to be descended, to descend, to originate</li>
<li>to spring, to arise, to result, to take place</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:произрастающий.html>произраста́ющий</a> (22226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:происки.html>про́иски</a> (16949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происки.html>про́иски</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">próiski</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:происки.html>про́исков</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>intrigues, scheming, underhand plotting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сорвать.html>сорва́ть</a> чьи́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:происки.html>про́иски</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sorvátʹ čʹí-libo <b>próiski</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">frustrate/foil smb's schemes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
